<span id="freeTextContainer11328091193831328758">* There is an English version of this book "Madonna in a fur coat"<br/><br/>I read this book with a lot of hesitation because it's so mainstream. Almost every serious reader seems to have read it. I too jumped on the bandwagon without realising how great a masterpiece I was about to encounter. This is one of the books which you start and finish in one go. While reading, I felt really close to Raif Efendi (the main character) and at some point we merged into one person and lived through his(our) life toget</span>
  <span id="freeText11328091193831328758" style="display:none">* There is an English version of this book "Madonna in a fur coat"<br /><br />I read this book with a lot of hesitation because it's so mainstream. Almost every serious reader seems to have read it. I too jumped on the bandwagon without realising how great a masterpiece I was about to encounter. This is one of the books which you start and finish in one go. While reading, I felt really close to Raif Efendi (the main character) and at some point we merged into one person and lived through his(our) life together. It was a very interesting adventure. Raif Efendi's experience of the banality of life until he found meaning for a very short time was predictably followed by a disastrous disappointment. All that was left to Raif Efendi was to spend the rest of his days dreaming and reimagining the few moments of peace he ever had. All-in-all an incredible portrayal of the human psyche.</span>

<div id="review_2573068265" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2573068265" />
    <a title="Liina Bachmann" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7310558-liina-bachmann"><img alt="Liina Bachmann" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537020610p2/7310558.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2573068265?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Liina Bachmann" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Liina Bachmann" href="/user/show/7310558-liina-bachmann">Liina Bachmann</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/27793819-madonna-in-a-fur-coat">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7310558-liina-bachmann?shelf=2018">2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2573068265" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5736109486820385341">This book could easily be the gold standard for melancholy love stories with unhappy endings. Set in 1920's Berlin winter it reeks of bittersweetness and missed opportunities. It really is a fur coat with a faint hint of Serge Lutens' "La Fille de Berlin", pale skin, snowstorms in empty streets, cold lonely pension rooms, the weight of the wait and cognac to keep one warm. A beautiful love story.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+Q6M5cBeRxzwIRkY8L0NFoIo8LSr4BkHJOeaUd8XV0jDKOU3ewCOdFcKrXkHSAfJVHcXfGVtl2B/mdzgElSl0g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vmF8RPkY+lPm2Cs7ga2SGEI8pUUXsI8Haig6k6r70ByERxWWQkYzO0Hzn1p2WJjHlGNCjdk9AWAxVnwiZ7gihg==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/116623.Sabahattin_Ali">About Sabahattin Ali</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/116623.Sabahattin_Ali"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1486602574p3/116623.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/116623.Sabahattin_Ali">Sabahattin Ali
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer11491213557716083525"><b>Sabahattin Ali</b> (February 25, 1907 – April 2, 1948) was a Turkish novelist, short-story writer, poet, and journalist.<br/><br/>He was born in 1907 in Eğridere township (now Ardino in southern Bulgaria) of the Sanjak of Gümülcine (now Komotini in northern Greece), in the Ottoman Empire. He lived in Istanbul, Çanakkale and Edremit before he entered the School of Education in Balıkesir. Then, he was transferred</span>
  <span id="freeText11491213557716083525" style="display:none"><b>Sabahattin Ali</b> (February 25, 1907 – April 2, 1948) was a Turkish novelist, short-story writer, poet, and journalist.<br /><br />He was born in 1907 in Eğridere township (now Ardino in southern Bulgaria) of the Sanjak of Gümülcine (now Komotini in northern Greece), in the Ottoman Empire. He lived in Istanbul, Çanakkale and Edremit before he entered the School of Education in Balıkesir. Then, he was transferred to the School of Education in Istanbul, where he graduated in 1926. After serving as a teacher in Yozgat for one year, he earned a fellowship from the Ministry of National Education and studied in Germany from 1928 to 1930. When he returned to Turkey, he taught German language in high schools at Aydın and Konya.<br /><br />While he was serving as a teacher in Konya, he was arrested for a poem he wrote criticizing Atatürk's policies, and accused of libelling two other journalists. Having served his sentence for several months in Konya and then in the Sinop Fortress Prison, he was released in 1933 in an amnesty granted to mark the 10th anniversary of the declaration of the Republic of Turkey. He then applied to the Ministry of National Education for permission to teach again. After proving his allegiance to Atatürk by writing the poem "Benim Aşkım" (literally: My Love or My Passion), he was assigned to the publications division at the Ministry of National Education. Sabahattin Ali married on May 16, 1935 and did his military service in 1936. He was imprisoned again and released in 1944. He also owned and edited a popular weekly newspaper called "Marko Paşa" (pronounced "Marco Pasha"), together with Aziz Nesin.<br /><br />Upon his release from prison, he suffered financial troubles. His application for a passport was denied. He was killed at the Bulgarian border, probably on 1 or 2 April 1948. His body was found on June 16, 1948. It is generally believed that he was killed by Ali Ertekin, a smuggler with connections to the National Security Service, who had been paid to help him pass the border.[2] Another hypothesis is that Ertekin handed him over to the security services, and he was killed during interrogation. It is believed he was killed because of his political opinions.<br /><br />Sabahattin Ali's 100th birth anniversary was celebrated in Bulgarian city Ardino in March 31, 2007. Ali is a well-known author in this country because his books have been read in schools in Bulgaria since 1950s.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11491213557716083525" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
